\title{QCRad methodology apply.}
\author{Natsis Athanasios}
\date{2023-01-25}

\begin{document}
\maketitle
\begin{abstract}
Data quality for radiation measurements as described by CN Long and Y Shi, September 2006, DOE/SC-ARM/TR-074. - The QCRad Value Added Product Surface Radiation Measurement Quality Control Testing Including Climatology\_Long2006.pdf
\end{abstract}

{
\hypersetup{linkcolor=}
\setcounter{tocdepth}{2}
\tableofcontents
}
\textbf{Source code: \href{https://github.com/thanasisn/RAD_QC}{github.com/thanasisn/RAD\_QC}}

\hypertarget{notes}{%
\subsubsection{Notes}\label{notes}}

Run for each year and apply Quality control on radiation data based on ID.

The chosen levels and filters have to be evaluated with the available data.

reads: QCRad\_LongShi\_v8\_id\_*

exports: TODO

- plot combination of flag for each point

\NormalTok{QS \textless{}{-}}\StringTok{ }\KeywordTok{list}\NormalTok{()}
\NormalTok{QS}\OperatorTok{$}\NormalTok{sun\_elev\_min     \textless{}{-}}\StringTok{   }\DecValTok{{-}2} \OperatorTok{*}\StringTok{ }\FloatTok{0.103} \CommentTok{\# 0. Drop all data when sun is below this point}
\NormalTok{QS}\OperatorTok{$}\NormalTok{sun\_elev\_no\_neg  \textless{}{-}}\StringTok{    }\DecValTok{0}         \CommentTok{\# 0. Don\textquotesingle{}t allow negative values below this sun angle}







\CommentTok{\#\#\#\#  1. PHYSICALLY POSSIBLE LIMITS PER BSRN  \#\#\#\#\#\#\#\#\#\#\#\#\#\#\#\#\#\#\#\#\#\#\#\#\#\#\#\#\#\#\#\#\#\#}

\newpage

\hypertarget{physically-possible-limits-per-bsrn}{%
\subsection{1. PHYSICALLY POSSIBLE LIMITS PER BSRN}\label{physically-possible-limits-per-bsrn}}

Test values are within physical/logical limits.

Direct upper constrain is a closeness to TSI at TOA. Shouldn't be any hits.
or need to remove data.

Global upper constrain is an modeled GHI value.

These limit should not be met, they are defined neat the maximum observed
values of the data set.

\begin{Shaded}
\begin{Highlighting}[]
\ControlFlowTok{if}\NormalTok{ (TEST\_}\DecValTok{01}\NormalTok{) \{}
    \KeywordTok{cat}\NormalTok{(}\KeywordTok{paste}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"}\CharTok{\textbackslash{}n}\StringTok{1. Physically Possible Limits.}\CharTok{\textbackslash{}n\textbackslash{}n}\StringTok{"}\NormalTok{))}

\NormalTok{    QS}\OperatorTok{$}\NormalTok{dir\_SWdn\_min \textless{}{-}}\StringTok{  }\DecValTok{{-}4}  \CommentTok{\# Minimum direct value to consider valid measurement}
\NormalTok{    QS}\OperatorTok{$}\NormalTok{dir\_SWdn\_dif \textless{}{-}}\StringTok{ }\DecValTok{327}  \CommentTok{\# Closeness to to TSI}
\NormalTok{    QS}\OperatorTok{$}\NormalTok{glo\_SWdn\_min \textless{}{-}}\StringTok{  }\DecValTok{{-}4}  \CommentTok{\# Minimum global value to consider valid measurement}
\NormalTok{    QS}\OperatorTok{$}\NormalTok{glo\_SWdn\_off \textless{}{-}}\StringTok{ }\DecValTok{160}  \CommentTok{\# Global departure offset above the model}
\NormalTok{    QS}\OperatorTok{$}\NormalTok{glo\_SWdn\_amp \textless{}{-}}\StringTok{ }\FloatTok{1.3}  \CommentTok{\# Global departure factor above the model}

    \CommentTok{\#\# . . Direct {-}{-}{-}{-}{-}{-}{-}{-}{-}{-}{-}{-}{-}{-}{-}{-}{-}{-}{-}{-}{-}{-}{-}{-}{-}{-}{-}{-}{-}{-}{-}{-}{-}{-}{-}{-}{-}{-}{-}{-}{-}{-}{-}{-}{-}{-}{-}{-}{-}{-}{-}{-}{-}{-}{-}{-}{-}{-}\#\#\#\#}
\NormalTok{    DATA[wattDIR }\OperatorTok{\textless{}}\StringTok{ }\NormalTok{QS}\OperatorTok{$}\NormalTok{dir\_SWdn\_min,}
\NormalTok{         QCF\_DIR\_}\DecValTok{01} \OperatorTok{:}\ErrorTok{=}\StringTok{ "Physical possible limit min (5)"}\NormalTok{]}
\NormalTok{    DATA[TSIextEARTH\_comb }\OperatorTok{{-}}\StringTok{ }\NormalTok{wattDIR }\OperatorTok{\textless{}}\StringTok{ }\NormalTok{QS}\OperatorTok{$}\NormalTok{dir\_SWdn\_dif,}
\NormalTok{         QCF\_DIR\_}\DecValTok{01} \OperatorTok{:}\ErrorTok{=}\StringTok{ "Physical possible limit max (6)"}\NormalTok{]}

    \CommentTok{\#\# . . Global {-}{-}{-}{-}{-}{-}{-}{-}{-}{-}{-}{-}{-}{-}{-}{-}{-}{-}{-}{-}{-}{-}{-}{-}{-}{-}{-}{-}{-}{-}{-}{-}{-}{-}{-}{-}{-}{-}{-}{-}{-}{-}{-}{-}{-}{-}{-}{-}{-}{-}{-}{-}{-}{-}{-}{-}{-}{-}\#\#\#\#}
\NormalTok{    DATA[wattGLB }\OperatorTok{\textless{}}\StringTok{ }\NormalTok{QS}\OperatorTok{$}\NormalTok{glo\_SWdn\_min,}
\NormalTok{         QCF\_GLB\_}\DecValTok{01} \OperatorTok{:}\ErrorTok{=}\StringTok{ "Physical possible limit min (5)"}\NormalTok{]}
\NormalTok{    DATA[, Glo\_max\_ref }\OperatorTok{:}\ErrorTok{=}\StringTok{ }\NormalTok{TSIextEARTH\_comb }\OperatorTok{*}\StringTok{ }\NormalTok{QS}\OperatorTok{$}\NormalTok{glo\_SWdn\_amp }\OperatorTok{*}\StringTok{ }\KeywordTok{cosde}\NormalTok{(SZA) }\OperatorTok{\^{}}\StringTok{ }\FloatTok{1.2} \OperatorTok{+}\StringTok{ }\NormalTok{QS}\OperatorTok{$}\NormalTok{glo\_SWdn\_off]}
\NormalTok{    DATA[wattGLB }\OperatorTok{\textgreater{}}\StringTok{ }\NormalTok{Glo\_max\_ref,}
\NormalTok{         QCF\_GLB\_}\DecValTok{01} \OperatorTok{:}\ErrorTok{=}\StringTok{ "Physical possible limit max (6)"}\NormalTok{]}

    \KeywordTok{cat}\NormalTok{(}\KeywordTok{pander}\NormalTok{(}\KeywordTok{table}\NormalTok{(DATA}\OperatorTok{$}\NormalTok{QCF\_DIR\_}\DecValTok{01}\NormalTok{, }\DataTypeTok{exclude =} \OtherTok{NULL}\NormalTok{)))}
    \KeywordTok{cat}\NormalTok{(}\KeywordTok{pander}\NormalTok{(}\KeywordTok{table}\NormalTok{(DATA}\OperatorTok{$}\NormalTok{QCF\_GLB\_}\DecValTok{01}\NormalTok{, }\DataTypeTok{exclude =} \OtherTok{NULL}\NormalTok{)))}
\NormalTok{\}}
\end{Highlighting}
\end{Shaded}

\hypertarget{extremely-rare-limits-per-bsrn}{%
\subsection{2. EXTREMELY RARE LIMITS PER BSRN}\label{extremely-rare-limits-per-bsrn}}

These should be a little more restrictive than 1. in order to start
catching erroneous values.

The choose of those settings may be optimized with an iterative process.

\begin{Shaded}
\begin{Highlighting}[]
\ControlFlowTok{if}\NormalTok{ (TEST\_}\DecValTok{02}\NormalTok{) \{}
    \KeywordTok{cat}\NormalTok{(}\KeywordTok{paste}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"}\CharTok{\textbackslash{}n}\StringTok{2. Extremely Rare Limits.}\CharTok{\textbackslash{}n\textbackslash{}n}\StringTok{"}\NormalTok{))}
    \CommentTok{\# Upper modeled values}
\NormalTok{    QS}\OperatorTok{$}\NormalTok{Dir\_SWdn\_amp     \textless{}{-}}\StringTok{    }\FloatTok{0.91} \CommentTok{\# Direct departure factor above the model}
\NormalTok{    QS}\OperatorTok{$}\NormalTok{Dir\_SWdn\_off     \textless{}{-}}\StringTok{ }\DecValTok{{-}140}    \CommentTok{\# Direct departure offset above the model}
\NormalTok{    QS}\OperatorTok{$}\NormalTok{Glo\_SWdn\_amp     \textless{}{-}}\StringTok{ }\FloatTok{1.18}    \CommentTok{\# Global departure factor above the model}
\NormalTok{    QS}\OperatorTok{$}\NormalTok{Glo\_SWdn\_off     \textless{}{-}}\StringTok{ }\DecValTok{40}      \CommentTok{\# Global departure offset above the model}
    \CommentTok{\# Minimum accepted values}
\NormalTok{    QS}\OperatorTok{$}\NormalTok{dir\_SWdn\_min\_ext \textless{}{-}}\StringTok{   }\DecValTok{{-}2}    \CommentTok{\# Extremely Rare Minimum Limits}
\NormalTok{    QS}\OperatorTok{$}\NormalTok{glo\_SWdn\_min\_ext \textless{}{-}}\StringTok{   }\DecValTok{{-}2}    \CommentTok{\# Extremely Rare Minimum Limits}
    \CommentTok{\# Compute reference values}
\NormalTok{    DATA[, Direct\_max }\OperatorTok{:}\ErrorTok{=}\StringTok{ }\NormalTok{TSIextEARTH\_comb }\OperatorTok{*}\StringTok{ }\NormalTok{QS}\OperatorTok{$}\NormalTok{Dir\_SWdn\_amp }\OperatorTok{*}\StringTok{ }\KeywordTok{cosde}\NormalTok{(SZA) }\OperatorTok{\^{}}\StringTok{ }\FloatTok{0.2} \OperatorTok{+}\StringTok{ }\NormalTok{QS}\OperatorTok{$}\NormalTok{Dir\_SWdn\_off]}
\NormalTok{    DATA[, Global\_max }\OperatorTok{:}\ErrorTok{=}\StringTok{ }\NormalTok{TSIextEARTH\_comb }\OperatorTok{*}\StringTok{ }\NormalTok{QS}\OperatorTok{$}\NormalTok{Glo\_SWdn\_amp }\OperatorTok{*}\StringTok{ }\KeywordTok{cosde}\NormalTok{(SZA) }\OperatorTok{\^{}}\StringTok{ }\FloatTok{1.2} \OperatorTok{+}\StringTok{ }\NormalTok{QS}\OperatorTok{$}\NormalTok{Glo\_SWdn\_off]}
    \CommentTok{\# Ignore too low values near horizon}
\NormalTok{    DATA[Direct\_max }\OperatorTok{\textless{}}\StringTok{ }\DecValTok{3}\NormalTok{, Direct\_max }\OperatorTok{:}\ErrorTok{=}\StringTok{ }\OtherTok{NA}\NormalTok{]}
\NormalTok{    DATA[Global\_max }\OperatorTok{\textless{}}\StringTok{ }\DecValTok{3}\NormalTok{, Direct\_max }\OperatorTok{:}\ErrorTok{=}\StringTok{ }\OtherTok{NA}\NormalTok{]}

    \CommentTok{\#\# . . Direct {-}{-}{-}{-}{-}{-}{-}{-}{-}{-}{-}{-}{-}{-}{-}{-}{-}{-}{-}{-}{-}{-}{-}{-}{-}{-}{-}{-}{-}{-}{-}{-}{-}{-}{-}{-}{-}{-}{-}{-}{-}{-}{-}{-}{-}{-}{-}{-}{-}{-}{-}{-}{-}{-}{-}{-}{-}{-}\#\#\#\#}
\NormalTok{    DATA[wattDIR }\OperatorTok{\textless{}}\StringTok{ }\NormalTok{QS}\OperatorTok{$}\NormalTok{dir\_SWdn\_min\_ext, QCF\_DIR\_}\DecValTok{02} \OperatorTok{:}\ErrorTok{=}\StringTok{ "Extremely rare limits min (3)"}\NormalTok{]}
\NormalTok{    DATA[wattDIR }\OperatorTok{\textgreater{}}\StringTok{ }\NormalTok{Direct\_max,          QCF\_DIR\_}\DecValTok{02} \OperatorTok{:}\ErrorTok{=}\StringTok{ "Extremely rare limits max (4)"}\NormalTok{]}

    \CommentTok{\# \#\# . . Global {-}{-}{-}{-}{-}{-}{-}{-}{-}{-}{-}{-}{-}{-}{-}{-}{-}{-}{-}{-}{-}{-}{-}{-}{-}{-}{-}{-}{-}{-}{-}{-}{-}{-}{-}{-}{-}{-}{-}{-}{-}{-}{-}{-}{-}{-}{-}{-}{-}{-}{-}{-}{-}{-}\#\#\#\#}
\NormalTok{    DATA[wattGLB }\OperatorTok{\textless{}}\StringTok{ }\NormalTok{QS}\OperatorTok{$}\NormalTok{glo\_SWdn\_min\_ext, QCF\_GLB\_}\DecValTok{02} \OperatorTok{:}\ErrorTok{=}\StringTok{ "Extremely rare limits min (3)"}\NormalTok{]}
\NormalTok{    DATA[wattGLB }\OperatorTok{\textgreater{}}\StringTok{ }\NormalTok{Global\_max,          QCF\_GLB\_}\DecValTok{02} \OperatorTok{:}\ErrorTok{=}\StringTok{ "Extremely rare limits max (4)"}\NormalTok{]}

    \KeywordTok{pander}\NormalTok{(}\KeywordTok{table}\NormalTok{(DATA}\OperatorTok{$}\NormalTok{QCF\_DIR\_}\DecValTok{02}\NormalTok{, }\DataTypeTok{exclude =} \OtherTok{TRUE}\NormalTok{))}
    \KeywordTok{pander}\NormalTok{(}\KeywordTok{table}\NormalTok{(DATA}\OperatorTok{$}\NormalTok{QCF\_GLB\_}\DecValTok{02}\NormalTok{, }\DataTypeTok{exclude =} \OtherTok{TRUE}\NormalTok{))}

\newpage

\hypertarget{climatological-configurable-limits}{%
\subsection{4. Climatological (configurable) Limits}\label{climatological-configurable-limits}}

Limits the maximum expected irradiance based on climatological
observations levels and the value of TSI.

Some hits on first limits are expected and need manual evaluation.

Hits on second limit should be problematic data.

For GHI this may limit the radiation enhancement cases.

Exclusions should be done case by case.

\begin{Shaded}

\hypertarget{rayleigh-limit-diffuse-comparison}{%
\subsection{6. Rayleigh Limit Diffuse Comparison}\label{rayleigh-limit-diffuse-comparison}}

Compare inferred diffuse radiation with a modeled value of diffuse,
based on SZA and atmospheric pressure.

The upper limit denotes no tracking of CHP-1.

Reasons:
- Difference on Sun observation angle due to different instruments location.
- Cases of instrument windows cleaning

\begin{Shaded}
\begin{Highlighting}[]
\ControlFlowTok{if}\NormalTok{ (TEST\_}\DecValTok{06}\NormalTok{) \{}
    \KeywordTok{cat}\NormalTok{(}\KeywordTok{paste}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"}\CharTok{\textbackslash{}n}\StringTok{6. Rayleigh Limit Diffuse Comparison.}\CharTok{\textbackslash{}n\textbackslash{}n}\StringTok{"}\NormalTok{))}
    \CommentTok{\# criteria}
\NormalTok{    QS}\OperatorTok{$}\NormalTok{Rayleigh\_upper\_lim \textless{}{-}}\StringTok{ }\DecValTok{500}   \CommentTok{\# Upper departure diffuse limit}
\NormalTok{    QS}\OperatorTok{$}\NormalTok{Rayleigh\_lower\_lim \textless{}{-}}\StringTok{  }\DecValTok{{-}3}   \CommentTok{\# Lower departure diffuse limit}

\NormalTok{    QS}\OperatorTok{$}\NormalTok{Rayleigh\_glo\_min   \textless{}{-}}\StringTok{  }\DecValTok{50}   \CommentTok{\# Low limit minimum global}
    \CommentTok{\# model}

        \KeywordTok{return}\NormalTok{( a }\OperatorTok{*}\StringTok{ }\NormalTok{mu\_}\DecValTok{0}     \OperatorTok{+}

\hypertarget{test-for-obstacles}{%
\subsection{7. Test for obstacles}\label{test-for-obstacles}}

\begin{verbatim}
NULL
\end{verbatim}

\begin{center}\rule{0.5\linewidth}{0.5pt}\end{center}

\newpage

\hypertarget{test-for-inverted-values}{%
\subsection{8. Test for inverted values}\label{test-for-inverted-values}}

Test the ratio of Diffuse / Global radiation.
When the Diffuse is too lower than Global, (less than a \% limit).

This denotes obstacles on the mornings mostly, or very low
signals when Sun is near the horizon.
Due to the time difference of sun shine, due to geometry, location and
obstacles.

And possible cases of Instrument windows cleaning shadowing.

Probably these value should be removed for CS when occurring on low
elevation angles, as the measurements can not be considered to reflect
the same condition of Sun visibility.

Additional criteria is needed for any data drop.

\begin{Shaded}

\newpage

\hypertarget{clearness-index-test}{%
\subsection{9. Clearness index test}\label{clearness-index-test}}

This filter is mine, and is applied on GHI data.

Data near elevation 0 are caused by the cos(SZA) while calculating
kt = GLB / (cos(sza) * TSI).

For larger elevation angles manual inspection is needed.

\begin{Shaded}
\begin{Highlighting}[]
\ControlFlowTok{if}\NormalTok{ (TEST\_}\DecValTok{09}\NormalTok{) \{}
    \KeywordTok{cat}\NormalTok{(}\KeywordTok{paste}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"}\CharTok{\textbackslash{}n}\StringTok{9. Clearness index (global/TSI) test.}\CharTok{\textbackslash{}n\textbackslash{}n}\StringTok{"}\NormalTok{))}

\NormalTok{    QS}\OperatorTok{$}\NormalTok{CL\_idx\_max \textless{}{-}}\StringTok{  }\FloatTok{1.13}  \CommentTok{\# Upper Clearness index accepted level}
\NormalTok{    QS}\OperatorTok{$}\NormalTok{CL\_idx\_min \textless{}{-}}\StringTok{ }\FloatTok{{-}0.001} \CommentTok{\# Lower Clearness index accepted level}
\NormalTok{    QS}\OperatorTok{$}\NormalTok{CL\_idx\_ele \textless{}{-}}\StringTok{  }\DecValTok{3}     \CommentTok{\# Apply for elevations above this angle}

    \CommentTok{\#\# . . Global {-}{-}{-}{-}{-}{-}{-}{-}{-}{-}{-}{-}{-}{-}{-}{-}{-}{-}{-}{-}{-}{-}{-}{-}{-}{-}{-}{-}{-}{-}{-}{-}{-}{-}{-}{-}{-}{-}{-}{-}{-}{-}{-}{-}{-}{-}{-}{-}{-}{-}{-}{-}{-}{-}{-}{-}{-}{-}\#\#\#\#}
\NormalTok{    DATA[Clearness\_Kt }\OperatorTok{\textgreater{}}\StringTok{ }\NormalTok{QS}\OperatorTok{$}\NormalTok{CL\_idx\_max }\OperatorTok{\&}\StringTok{ }\NormalTok{Elevat }\OperatorTok{\textgreater{}}\StringTok{ }\NormalTok{QS}\OperatorTok{$}\NormalTok{CL\_idx\_ele,}
\NormalTok{         QCF\_GLB\_}\DecValTok{09} \OperatorTok{:}\ErrorTok{=}\StringTok{ "Clearness index limit max (19)"}\NormalTok{ ]}
\NormalTok{    DATA[Clearness\_Kt }\OperatorTok{\textless{}}\StringTok{ }\NormalTok{QS}\OperatorTok{$}\NormalTok{CL\_idx\_min }\OperatorTok{\&}\StringTok{ }\NormalTok{Elevat }\OperatorTok{\textgreater{}}\StringTok{ }\NormalTok{QS}\OperatorTok{$}\NormalTok{CL\_idx\_ele,}
\NormalTok{         QCF\_GLB\_}\DecValTok{09} \OperatorTok{:}\ErrorTok{=}\StringTok{ "Clearness index limit min (20)"}\NormalTok{ ]}

    \KeywordTok{cat}\NormalTok{(}\KeywordTok{pander}\NormalTok{(}\KeywordTok{table}\NormalTok{(DATA}\OperatorTok{$}\NormalTok{QCF\_GLB\_}\DecValTok{09}\NormalTok{, }\DataTypeTok{exclude =} \OtherTok{TRUE}\NormalTok{)))}
